VM18 injected.js:27 [Mr Blue Analysis]: üîç Root Cause: The React.Children.only function is expecting a single React element child, but it's receiving multiple children or no children at all.

‚öôÔ∏è Auto-fixable: No

üéØ Severity: High

üìù Fix Steps:
1. Check the component that's using React.Children.only and ensure it's only rendering a single child element.
2. Verify that the child element is a valid React element and not a primitive value like a string or number.
3. If the component needs to render multiple children, consider using React.Fragment or an array of React elements instead of React.Children.only.


üíª Code Snippet:
React.Children.only(<div>Single Child</div>)



üìñ Explanation:
React.Children.only is a utility function that helps ensure a component only renders a single child element. If your component needs to render multiple children, you'll need to modify it to use a different approach.
